Keywords: 
chairman states existing 

Final sequence: 

Mr. Chairman, I make a point of order against the amendment because it proposes to change existing law and constitutes legislation in an appropriations bill; therefore it violates clause 2 of rule XXI and the rules of the House. The rule states in pertinent part that a general debate shall be limited to the amendment offered and that any Member seeking to offer an amendment shall be limited to the number of committee Chairman or ranking minority member designated in the report. The rule further provides that the amendments should be relevant to the subject matter covered by the amendment and should be relevant to existing law. The rule further provides that no amendments may be in order if they change existing law or are related to the subject matter covered by the amendment or proposed amendment, and that debate on such amendments shall be limited to 60 minutes.  I ask for a ruling from the Chair.  The CHAIRMAN. Does any other Member wish to be heard on the point of order?
